Mr. Moon's Selected Words
60
Mr. Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Path That the Family Must Follow
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is the first day of August 1972. Father, from today until the remaining five months of this year, please align this nation and this world with the direction of Your providence. Allow these coming months to be a time when we can meet the moment of fulfillment in the historical course that has been so painstakingly guided by You.
Father, today is a new month and a new morning, so please especially love this nation and this people. We have gathered here with hearts that are concerned about Your remaining will for restoration, longing for this nation to be one that brings joy to Heaven, that can be governed by Heaven, and that can receive Heaven's blessings. Please allow our unity to be in accordance with Your will.
We know well that the path You walk is one that we must follow throughout our lives. When we think about the mission of restoration that You have left behind, which connects from the individual to the family, nation, and world, we realize that the true individuals, families, nations, and worlds You seek are far from the standards we envision. The more we reflect on ourselves, who long for Heaven and follow for Heaven, the more we feel our inadequacies and shortcomings.
August 1, 1972 (Tuesday), Namsan Holy Ground.
* This message was published in the 46th issue of the <Newsletter> under the title "Let Us Be Filial Sons Who Can Be Hopes and Strengths Before Our Parents."
8   The Path That the Family Must Follow
However, when we see that there are no groups on this earth who know Your will and the direction of Your providence, the more we understand that there remains a heavenly mission that must be established through them, the more we realize that You alone are the one who is pitiful, and that the one who must bear the burdens of the arduous path of suffering is only Heaven.
Father! You who always labor for Your pitiful children! In our hearts, we pursue the path You walk, and with our bodies, we wish to walk the path of loyalty and filial piety before Your will.
You have led these people thus far, so may they continue to match their steps with You, helping to pioneer a foundation for Your glory and becoming children who can cooperate with Your heart.
Father! Although the history of the Unification Church is short, the heritage and tradition that have been passed down have come down together with the history of humanity's ancestors. The history woven by those ancestors is not a history of joy but a history of sorrow, and every time we think of this, Father, we feel even more deeply the weight of our mission.
It is our mission and duty to comfort and serve the Father who has come forth with historical sorrow, and we must fulfill our responsibilities with all our intellect and filial piety, but we must also deeply feel how great Your sorrow is as You look upon our unworthy selves who cannot always stand in such a position.
For this reason, we know well that we cannot go forth with our own self but must praise Your authority and look upon the path of suffering as we go.
Father, please accept our inadequate hearts that always wish for Your day of victory, and bless us so that we can embrace this nation, this people, and this world in Your bosom.
Father, today is especially the first day of August. Father! I have mentioned here before that the latter half of this year is important, and from now on, this nation and this people must become one. We must be united from the individual level, from the family level. All families must devote all their sincerity for the nation and for the unification of the North and South, and we feel that we are in a national era where this must be done. Therefore, we must be the examples who know that Heaven must not depart from here. We, who bear the name of family, must be completely united. Thus, we must feel that we have an important responsibility to make a decisive appeal before the global mission.
We know that a person does not live long on this earth. We also know that no matter how great a desire one has on this earth, one cannot achieve everything according to that desire. We understand that we have no choice but to go, fight, pioneer, and run along with the desires and will that Heaven hopes for.
When we are with Heaven, even if we fall along the way, we will not perish; and when we fight with Heaven, even if we die, we will not truly die, so please remember the children of unification.
Moreover, please protect the frontline members. They are not only in Korea but are spread throughout the world, and wherever they go, Your authority and presence must be revealed. Please honor Heaven's dignity. Please reveal Heaven's will. Thus, may they become a group of children who can set a new standard before humanity and clearly present the direction that humanity must go in the future.
For this purpose, we entrust the history of the coming years of 1972 to You, Father, so please guide it. When we think that we must fulfill the mission of being the locomotive that pulls not only for one nation but for all humanity, we feel the weight of the entrusted responsibility, yet we also know that our strength is insufficient and that we cannot do it with our own power, so we hold onto our faith in Heaven.
When we think of Your difficulties, we can overcome even the hardest situations. We know the historical fact that when we resolve to walk together with You, who have come through the path of suffering and whose death crossed paths with the martyrs' legacy, Heaven has protected us, opened the way for us, and safeguarded everything.
10   The Path That the Family Must Follow
Father! We must become a group that You can protect. We must become a group that You can guide directly to be victors. To do this, we must start from You and conclude with You, and when we think of this principle, please look upon our insufficiencies and shortcomings. Please guide us to be established in the form that You desire. Allow us to strive so that we may not lack in receiving Your protection on this final battlefield.
We earnestly wish for You to grant us all the strength we can muster.
When the heart of Heaven's compassion rests upon our lives, when it stays in the path we walk or in the course of our lives, we know that these will become a group that can leave a foundation of victory on this earth amidst shining hope. We have learned through principles that living for oneself leads to dead ends. We must run for public purposes. Now, we must run through this August.
Please remember the young children who are fighting on the front lines. They have not come forth for anyone's grievances but for Your grievances. We were born into hardship and have walked the path of suffering, so even if we cannot escape from the path of suffering, we have no regrets. Our only wish is to relieve Your grievances and lessen Your suffering, so if we have started because of You, let the process be the same. The results must also be so.
If we have spent our youth on such a path, then surely our adulthood and old age will follow, and we are well aware that if we do not fulfill our mission in this lifetime, we must leave a legacy for our descendants to achieve the fulfillment of historical missions.
Father! We know that a group that sincerely yearns for Heaven and offers all their devotion before Heaven will not perish. Please do not let the movements of Heaven's compassion around us depart. We seek the grace of Heaven to dwell in the places where we stay. Every time this happens, we know that that place, that gathering, and that movement will progress.
Father! You who have guided the Unification Church until now! The owner of this place is no one but You. You alone can lead all the leaders and groups here. We have followed You thus far, knowing this, and we continue to go, knowing this, and we are now looking forward to victory in accordance with the way of obedience.
Where there is victory, we know that there is nothing to boast about because nothing has been achieved by us. It is all because of You, so we return it to You, and if You grant us grace, we will gratefully receive it, and if You do not grant it, we will not keep that grace for ourselves but will ask that it be left for a greater nation and world, believing that the children who carry this heart will walk the path of victory and glory together.
Father, now from this first day of the month, please bless this month. This month is a complex month. It is the first day of August, which marks a new starting point. 1972 has been called the peak year in the historical age. We have passed July. Please allow new hopes to dwell from August. Please allow hope to find its way onto this nation, this people, and this land from August. Please let the sound of liberation and freedom ring out before humanity, which is currently in distress and tribulation. Father, we earnestly wish and desire this.
Please bless this month, and as we serve for this month, if there are days of service offered before Heaven during this month, we earnestly wish and desire that those days be remembered as days of pride.
Father, please look upon the children gathered here with compassion. We have nothing. We may be a pitiful group in the world, but let us be a group that knows how to love You even more in our pitiful state. We know that even if we work hard and do not receive recognition for our efforts on this earth, You alone recognize us. The more we realize this, the more we must exalt You. We must recognize how grateful and awe-inspiring it is to be able to call You Father when we are lonely.
12   The Path That the Family Must Follow
We must understand that a group that knows You well and can discuss matters with You, even if they are in the most lonely, pitiful, and miserable positions, are truly happy people compared to those who are in a position of ignorance, groaning and worrying about their lives.
Father, please bless our families. Please raise the children born in those families for Your will. Thus, we earnestly ask and desire that they be dedicated to You and become precious ones who can inherit Your nation and Your world for future generations.
This place is the central holy ground connecting 120 holy sites. Father, please allow the many people looking toward this Namsan, the many citizens of Seoul, to look up to Heaven. Please grant the citizens of this central place of the nations the spiritual gifts to pursue Your desires and ideals in their hearts. May the many groups coming to Seoul feel in their hearts what Heaven's timing is, and if there are those who cannot do so, please allow them to have the heart to reassess themselves before the path ahead.
Father, in a few days, there will be a gathering centered around Seoul where the North and South will meet, so please be the master among them. Please guide this nation and this people to be able to bow before Your will in the future. We earnestly wish and desire that this nation, with its thirty million people, can look to Heaven with nothing to possess and with a childlike heart, knowing how to embrace Heaven's bosom.
Please allow the days and months after today to be days of pride, and we earnestly ask that the victories of Heaven be built upon the second seven-year course.
Through the holy sites connected with Korea, Japan, the United States, Germany, and 40 other countries, we earnestly ask that many people’s hearts, which admire the new morning of peace, may sprout together with the desires that Heaven wishes.
Please allow everything to be governed within Your providence. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.
13
<Words> As you all know, we are members of the Unification Church. When we say "family," of course, the roles assigned may differ, but in terms of the path we take and the emotions we live with, we cannot have different life courses regardless of our environment or circumstances. If there is a father and children, even if the work they do is different, in the emotional realm of life, it is the same. When the father is sad, the children, although in different positions, must feel the sadness to truly be regarded as the children of that parent.
The Concept of Family Different from the World
From this perspective, we, the members of the Unification Church, say "We are family," and the path that the family must follow, while certainly aligned with the purpose of the will, must also not differ in emotional life.
Moreover, when the family is in a position of hardship, that family must become one. When the parents are in sorrow, the children and family members living together will also be engulfed in that sorrow.
To resolve that sorrow, one must not stand in a position that prioritizes their own responsibilities or the importance of their work. When one does so, they cannot be said to be standing in unity with their parents. From there, emotional life cannot be separated. However, even if the external circumstances are very different, if one can cast aside all that and, even if those things disappear, become one heart and one mind with the parents, feeling the same pain in body and spirit regarding the sorrow being endured, then even if that family has nothing and cannot do anything, and has nothing to boast about, a new beginning of pride can start from here. From here, one can choose a different path than ever before.
is. When we resolve to move forward from there, we come to understand that a new path can be sought, even if it means crossing a line.

14 The Original Path for Family Members
We often refer to each other as family. When we consider this in relation to family, it is needless to say that the sorrow of parents is significant, but on the other hand, the sorrow of children is not solely their own. The sorrow of children is directly connected to the sorrow of their parents. Regardless of how many children or family members there are, that is not the issue. When one person among many family members experiences sorrow, the entire family encompasses that one person's sorrow. They become integrated into it. Centered around sorrow, they become one rather than two. That unity is the pride of that family, the strength of that family, and the source of life for that family, which we come to realize.

If we think of the sorrow of one family member only as that person's sorrow, and if all ten family members think that way, then those ten family members cannot become one. Even if those ten family members hope for peace, happiness, or rest in their hearts, there can be no rest among them. If any individual seeks rest, whatever they find as personal rest cannot serve as a foundation for the rest of the whole. If ten people each find their own personal refuge in their self-interest, that becomes the foundation of mutual anxiety and the root of discord or unhappiness, which we clearly understand through our lives and the stories surrounding our family members.

When we consider this content from the perspective of family, we are different from families in the general world. A family in the world can find happiness by living together throughout their lives, supporting one another, and being a source of comfort, as they seek a path of happiness together. Thus, they may become a family that can boast more than anyone else in their lives. However, the concept of family that we speak of is different. It is not centered on the world but centered on heaven. It is centered on the Heavenly Parent. It is centered on the Heavenly Father. That Heavenly Parent is not a parent who governs a temporary era. They are the parents who dominate and govern history, who rule and oversee this era. Furthermore, they are the parents who must govern the future era as well.

When we think again about having such a Heavenly Parent, we come to realize that the Heavenly Parent is dealing with fallen humanity. We understand that we ourselves have not yet achieved complete liberation within that fallen realm.

Humans Must Find a Way for God to Rest
In this light, the question of what kind of place can allow the Heavenly Parent to rest with joy, and through which person that place will be realized, becomes a most serious issue. We know that there are not many who can confidently answer 'yes' when asked if the Heavenly Parent can rest and find a path to rest through themselves.

So, who should prepare the way for heaven's rest, and who should indicate this direction? We know that for fallen beings like us, it is nearly impossible. The more we think about it, the more we realize that if there is one wish we can have as fallen humans, it is to provide a foundation for heaven's rest and to take responsibility for pointing out the direction of that rest. This is an undeniable conclusion.

From this perspective, if the heart that heaven has decided upon is joyful and can rest, how wonderful it would be if that heaven were a heaven that could burn with firm conviction. However, heaven has not been able to find the path of happiness from the very beginning. Heaven has experienced more unhappiness, lamentation, and suffering than joy and rest. In other words, from the day humanity's ancestors began, they brought not rest but destruction, not happiness but unhappiness.

If the issues that arose could be resolved through our human stories, it would be simple, but the unhappiness that has arisen cannot be resolved with the stories humans tell. If this were something that could be resolved with heaven's authority, it might be different, but it is not something that God can resolve with that authority.

We know that the subject who must resolve these issues is heaven, yet heaven stands in a position where it cannot resolve them.

In other words, due to the fall, the standard of true humanity has been lost, and the standard of the true God has also been lost. When we look at the original principles, God's authority and human authority were established in a position where they could rightfully dominate Satan. God's happiness, God's rest, and the happiness that humans envision must be pursued from a position of authority that can dominate Satan, from a position even higher than that. When we think about this, we realize that humanity has not risen to that higher position.

Therefore, even though heaven has thought about and understood the concept of rest until now, there is no place where heaven can say it will rest. Thus, we understand that heaven has not been able to emerge from the path of providence, having established some decisive boundary line where it can rest.

Heaven hoped for this during Noah's time, but it ended in failure. The same was true during Abraham's time, and it continued through the times of Moses and Jesus. When we consider that the history that has traced such a position has not been a history affirming heaven's wishes and joy, but rather a history that has compounded sorrow, the question of where heaven's desired rest and happiness might be becomes a most serious issue.

From this perspective, since the fall was caused by humans, it is a problem that humans must take responsibility for. A person with the heart to comfort heaven before heaven can rest is needed. Rather than humans seeking the direction for heaven's rest, they must stand before heaven and introduce the path through which heaven can rest, and find the place of rest. It is not God who seeks; it is humans who must seek. It is not God who pioneers; it is humans who must pioneer.

We, who should be catalysts for filial piety
Humanity finds itself in the position of a son who has been unfilial to the parent. The very ones who have caused unhappiness are us humans. Because we have committed unspeakable acts of unfiliality before heaven, in order for an unfilial person to stand before heaven with dignity, they must have a position of being a filial child.

To reflect on all that has been unhappy and unfilial, one must return to their original heart and see the heart of the parent who has grieved, rather than simply looking at the mistakes of unfilial acts. Only by becoming a child who can feel sorrow beyond that can the child who has been unhappy and unfilial find a way to heal the heart of the parent who has been hurt by their unfiliality.

When we look at it this way, what should we, who have embarked on the path of unfiliality and have sown the seeds of unhappiness, do before our Heavenly Parent? While it is certainly important to pursue our own rest and walk the path of our own rest, how much pain has heaven suffered because we have made it unhappy and become unfilial children? Therefore, the question is how we can comfort that heart.

Heaven knows that we humans stand in a limited position. We do not believe that we are qualified to behold the glory of God, who is all-powerful. We are seen as pitiful beings deserving of sympathy.

That is why we cannot stand in a position where we can make excuses. We cannot make excuses. When we look at the divine countenance, even though we have been branded as unfilial children, there is no other way but to kneel before the parent, shedding tears, and confessing our sins that have caused harm to the parent.

Thus, we, who have inherited the history of unfiliality that has wounded the heart of the parent, what excuse can we make before heaven, and how can we stand firm and say that we can comfort heaven? It cannot be done.

The more we understand history, the more we must cover heaven's grievances with tears, and we must walk a path more miserable than that of the father. When such a scene occurs, a new sympathy from heaven will begin here. However, if one shamelessly makes excuses for themselves and claims to have their own perspective, there can be no sympathy or new connections.

We are beings who deserve to die a thousand times, and appearing before you is a torment. Calling your name and looking at your divine countenance feels more miserable than death. If I can leave behind even a single condition to comfort your wounded heart, I have no greater wish. Standing in a position similar to that of a desperate person, someone without hope who cannot look at anyone in the world, can evoke a new meaning of heaven's sympathy, and it is only in that path that a new historical beginning can be connected. It is not about thinking of oneself, one’s pride or face, one’s past experiences, or one’s current position; these are not the issues.

We, the members of the Unification Church, claim that we have sworn to become filial children of heaven. We must calmly analyze and critique once more. How much have my hands become the hands of a filial child that heaven longs for? How much has my face become the appearance of a filial child that heaven can long for?

When we consider how much my being has become a catalyst for filial piety, overcoming any adversity day or night, and how much I have been able to reflect the image of the father who strives to pave the way for filial children, we find that we cannot have confidence in ourselves.

These hands and this appearance, along with all the history of the past, are filled with unfiliality, overflowing with it. We have been the ones who drove nails into God's heart. Yet, we complained and whined.

In this sense, standing here on this first day of August, we have a desire to be filial children for heaven. We have a desire to walk the path of loyalty. However, before that desire, what is most precious is how I can become a sacrificial offering of sympathy before heaven and maintain that position.

To find the path of happiness, one must stand in the position of sacrifice.
We hope for unification. We hope to become one. While it is easy to become one and show sympathy when centered on work, we know it is difficult to become one when centered on the heart. More than that, when it comes to emotional issues, it becomes even more challenging, doesn’t it? When we consider this, we can say that becoming one centered on work is rebirth, becoming one centered on the heart is growth, and becoming one centered on the heart is completion.

In the matter of becoming one centered on the heart, one cannot be in a position of being there for oneself. For family members to achieve the motivation for peace and to be a source of comfort for one another, they must stand in the position of being there for each other. Only from the position of being there for you, being there for family members, can that peace be envisioned. When parents are there for their children, only then does the place of comfort for the children begin. When parents are there for themselves, the place of comfort and happiness for the children becomes a place of destruction.

Similarly, if children before their parents say, “The parents are here for me, and I am here for myself,” then there can be no place of rest and happiness for those parents. The more people think this way, the more unhappy it becomes, and this cannot serve as a foundation for rest. In other words, only when family members are there for other family members can it become a foundation for peace, a place of rest, and conditions for happiness.

From there, if we take responsibility for family members, sacrifice more, and stand in a position where we take on the sorrows of the whole as our own and the difficulties of the whole as our own, then the happiness of that family begins.

Even if the parents cannot do so, even if the siblings cannot do so, if there is one person who is prepared to sacrifice and take responsibility for the whole, then the conditions for happiness begin because of that one person.

When we look at it this way, if we see humanity as the children of God centered on heaven and earth, then when God is in a position to be there for us, those children cannot find the path of happiness.

We do not see heaven as being there for itself or fighting for itself until now. Heaven has fought for humanity, just as parents are there for their children. When we think about the countless sufferings that heaven has embraced and fought through day by day, we realize that heaven is always noble. Heaven is powerful. Heaven is always someone we look up to. Heaven is always someone we want to serve. We always want to become one with heaven. However, if heaven stands in a position of being there only for itself, then there is no unity or anything else with that heaven, and all reverence and respect for such a heaven will fade away.

Heaven is love beyond measure. Before such a heaven, humanity, standing in the position of children today, includes countless nations and ethnicities. Among those countless nations, we must ask what individuals, families, clans, or nations have claimed to be there for heaven, for the sake of heaven. We realize that none exist.

Looking at Jesus, the reason he could introduce the path of happiness before heaven and provide a new hope was because he prayed, “Not my will, but yours be done.” When Jesus prayed that, it was a moment of breathlessness where he resolved to die for the sake of heaven’s well-being. He stood on the thought that “dying for heaven’s well-being is the path of filial piety. That can bring about the conditions for the place of rest and happiness and serve as a foundation for saving families.”

When we look at the entire concept of the chosen people, we see that when such thoughts remain, that nation has developed. Furthermore, when we consider the rise and fall of nations, that country has prospered when the ruler and the people have become one.
It speaks of the people. When such people gather and live together, we know that the nation must have awakened its history. In this light, we are now leaving behind decades of history.

**Pride that Leads to Greater Misfortune**

August 15 marks the 27th anniversary of liberation. In light of this issue, was there truly a unified point centered around the Unification Church? That is the question. This year, we have come out with the vast slogan of "Defending the Unification Front." The boundary of this defense does not refer to the limits of one's own self. It speaks of the grave mission of a nation becoming a boundary that must defend the world beyond the nation.

So, what must be defended first? Is it the land? If heaven is attacked from the land, then heaven will directly retaliate. The purpose is to defend the world, to prevent damage in the global providence. It is to pave the way to establish a foundation of rest in God's heart for the world.

In light of this issue, heaven may seem distant and unrelated to me, but that is not the case. Heaven is exceedingly close. It is closer than your own cells. God is the center of your entire being. Therefore, He manages you, who are the counterpart. The counterpart cannot move on its own. Even when considering the solar system, the nine planets do not manage the sun; rather, the planets revolve around the sun while forgetting it.

In the same way, because God is the center of our entirety, and we ourselves are in a relative position where we cannot manage the center, it is easy to forget that center. However, it is not the case that the planets revolve because they forget the sun; rather, the sun exists, and because it exists, the planets revolve.

The center of our existence is God. I am not revolving while observing and managing that center. Am I not in the same position as the planets of the solar system, which revolve around their own center while following a certain orbit? The sun is stationary in one place. If it were to move, the universe would be thrown into chaos and face destruction.

In this light, there is heaven, our center. However, while revolving, we should be following the principles and revolving in the same direction centered on heaven, yet we are revolving in the opposite direction. The fact that we are revolving in the opposite direction is a minus for both ourselves and the subject. Heaven, which looks upon this world, cannot be at ease. Heaven cannot be at ease.

When I see members going out to evangelize and becoming disheartened due to hardships, I ask, for whom did they start? From whom did they begin, and for whom is the process, and whose purpose are they trying to achieve? This is undoubtedly a betrayal. It proves that they started for themselves, sought their own interests in the process, and if the purpose is achieved, they claim it as theirs. Such beings are not needed by heaven. In such a state, the more the purpose is achieved, the more unfilial they become. It leads to greater tragedy. Such individuals cannot be left alone by heaven. They are eliminated.

For this reason, heaven's providence has never used those who bring pride in any era, even if heaven suffers, even if it brings immense obstacles to the providential will. Why is that? Because it leads to greater misfortune.

**Following the Path of Parents is the Duty of Children**

Our Unification Church has walked the path of suffering. We have walked a difficult path. It was not for the teacher, but for the nation and the world. Moreover, it was for God. It was for God and God's will. When we speak of God's will, it is not just for my individual self. It is for the will of God, and thus that path still remains. Even now, there are members of our Unification Church who risk their lives on the front lines for the world. There are members fighting underground, in dark worlds, risking their lives. In other words, there are members standing at the global forefront. Some fight on behalf of their country, while others fight for their own tribes.

Then, if we are to sympathize, whom should we sympathize with? Should we not sympathize more with those who fight for something greater than those who fight for their tribes or nations, that is, those who fight on the path of death for the world? Suppose there are two children; one is sick and about to die, and the other is drowning. The sick child has come to the point of death after a long suffering, while the drowning child is in immediate danger of losing their life. The parent would not say, "Oh, I should save my son who has suffered for a long time first." In the path of life and death, the parent would want to save the child who is in immediate danger of death. In this light, it is the principle to sympathize with, support, and unite for those who stand on the front lines sacrificing their lives, isn’t it?

If you work for your tribe, you should not think, "Ah, I am working for my tribe, but the church does not recognize it. The church must unite. All members of the Unification Church should cooperate with me as the center." That kind of thinking is wrong. If it is for the nation, you must cooperate centered on the nation. That is a different position.

Then, it is just and will become the tradition of this world for the entire nation to unite and cooperate for those who are on the front lines, ready to sacrifice their lives with a greater responsibility. In light of this issue, if one gives up their environment just because they are having a hard time and makes excuses for themselves, if God exists, they are a shocking betrayer of God. Isn’t that so?

We have fought this far. Now, our time is drawing near, and the moment of whether we can overcome the peak of normalcy is approaching us. At such a time, what should we unite around? We must unite around the heart, centered on the heart and feelings, rather than uniting around work.

Then, what is God centered on in His progress? We must put all our sincerity into that center. What path is heaven taking? If there is a path it is taking, we should be concerned about that path, even if I take a different path. As children, we should be concerned about the path that our parents are taking, the path that our mother and father are taking. Even if we live in different places, our daily lives should be in harmony with that heart, and we should live in a place where our heart aligns with heaven. Isn’t that the proper step that heaven’s family should take? In light of these issues, today, you should not become betrayers in front of the name of family. You should not become betrayers in reality.

In this sense, we must once again mark this beginning of August... It is time for you to make a new start after joining the Unification Church. The joy you felt when you first entered the church should not fade away. If it has become a seed that was sown in a normal way, it should bear fruit and harvest dozens or hundreds of seeds, and if those seeds are sown again, shouldn’t we welcome dozens or hundreds of spring days? A single flower blooming in a desolate landscape should create a flower garden with many flowers and produce a fragrant garden that spreads many fragrances. Are you in such a fruitful garden that can emit such fragrances? That is not the case.

Liking the fragrance I emit alone is lonely. However, the fragrance I emit among many fragrances is noble. It becomes a condition where the public can dwell and all things can harmonize. However, being alone is lonely and desolate.

**God Who Values Public Principles**

In this light, when you enter the church and start as one person, if you remain in the same state without branching out, sprouting leaves, or blooming flowers, and end up in a hopeless position, who will sympathize with that person? No one can sympathize. It would be better to uproot and replant them. Such things happen in the world, but heaven is the same. Heaven desires perfection. Heaven seeks not individual perfection but a perfect representation of the whole. In light of this issue, it is serious.

If you have had a heartfelt experience after entering the church, that is not the standard of completion. It is not the standard of completion but a beginning. It is rebirth. If you have formed a heartfelt bond with the teacher on a flat level, that bond belongs to rebirth. Centered on this rebirth, through heaven and the growth process, by establishing subjectivity through your own subjectivity before all people, when all people can finally stand in that heartfelt authority, that becomes the realm of completion. Completion is achieved centered on this earth, this land.

When you enter the Unification Church, what you resolve is of a rebirth nature. You may rejoice, saying, "I have now found my purpose, which I did not know in the world of death, where there was no purpose or value in life." However, that is limited to yourself.

However, when you bear the name of a member, you must realize that you are not alone. After you resolve and enter, you are not alone. It is not according to my will or my desires. From that point on, my desires and the desires of my family become the desires of being a member.

In this light, the desires of the family refer to seeking happiness that aligns with the emotional world centered on the parents, not seeking misfortune. We must unite centered on God.

Then, have you truly united as members in the true sense after entering the church? That is the question. If you have experienced the pain of seeing your siblings or parents struggle at home, have you felt that even more among our members? They are pitiful people. Why are they pitiful? They have no home. Though they are called family, they have no home, no relatives, and no nation. However, in the world, there are homes and nations. In this light, who is more pitiful? We, who stand in a public position, are more pitiful. For this reason, heaven will love us. Even if it cannot love the world, because we stand in such a position, God, who values public principles, loves us while leaving the world behind.

**Facing the Time to Pray All Night**

Now, in that regard, what position are we in? The house you live in is not your house. The connections made centered on the teacher did not happen in our country. When viewed centered on God, it did not happen in God's courtyard but within the enemy's barbed wire. Therefore, we must unite and break through this barbed wire. Individual barbed wires block us, as do family barbed wires, tribal barbed wires, national barbed wires, and world barbed wires, so we must break through these.

To do this, we cannot do it alone. To break through the family barbed wire, the husband and wife must unite. To break through the tribal barbed wire, the family must unite, and to break through the national barbed wire, the tribe must unite, and to break through the national barbed wire, the South Korean nation must unite.

Now is the time for North and South Korea, which are in opposing positions, to meet and seek a unified plan. The question of who is more strongly united will determine the leadership of unification.

Then, we must hope to unite strongly centered on God's will, more than any group. This goes without saying. We are in such a time.

For this reason, we must welcome a new spring where we can long for each other as family members. In the past, when going out to evangelize and feeling lonely, there are stories of members traveling 50 ri to meet a lonely member halfway, right? At that time, it was a time of distinguishing individuals, but now it is time to go toward the nation. In such a time, if you have the desire to do so, you should have the heart to seek out the members around you, not just once but ten times, in order to have the name of a normal Unification Church member.

On one side, it must be centered on that side, and on one path, it must be centered on that path. Furthermore, it is not enough for just your path to go well. For the entire path to go well, you must do things that can serve as an example before the whole path. In being that example, it is not centered on yourself. You must become an example according to the will of the family and the will of the parents. In doing so, you will become a filial child who shines more and more.

Uniting around the truth of the Unification Church is an easy task. It is easy to unite with words. However, substantive unity is difficult.

Today, when we look at this land, we know that it has woven a tragic history without being able to unite even centered on the truth. If that is the case, is it not difficult to unite even centered on words and truth? Unification Church members say, "I am a principle person," centered on the principle, and claim to be united. That is not the problem. The content must be united. In other words, the hearts must be united. Furthermore, we must become filial children and loyal subjects. That will not be easy.

In this sense, you must understand that the path of filial piety required of us after August has providential significance. Now you must live a life fulfilling the duties of filial piety in a providential sense. Is it not a time that no one has matched?

Now, as a leader centered on heaven's will, when we exert all our efforts to shout, hasn’t the time come when that shout can reach not only the earth but also heaven? It is better than the time of Jesus. Jesus prayed all night in the Garden of Gethsemane, but there was no response to his three prayers. There was no response from the nation or the Jewish church, but our time is different. When I step forward, prepared for death, there are many who can respond beyond the nation and to the world. We are in such a time.

Therefore, even if we stay up all night, we must do so for our members. The one who stays up all night for themselves becomes like Peter. Wasn’t it Jesus’ position to stay up all night for the nation and the world?
Death comes to obscure the path, and in such a fateful journey, what he was concerned about was not his own death but the well-being of his disciples and his nation. That is why divine compassion descended upon him, and perhaps that is why he was resurrected. You must understand this. The time is now.

Now is the time for our Unification Church to pray just as Jesus did when he spent the night in prayer at the Garden of Gethsemane. As we pray through the night, it is not the time to pray for ourselves. We must pray for our nation and for all of humanity. Those who stay up all night for that purpose and weep together for it will not perish. Those who have resolved to walk the path of death together will not perish. That critical path will deliver the final judgment that promises resurrection. It will not lead to our destruction; rather, it will provide the motivation for life that can urge resurrection. Such an era is approaching us.

Above all, the internal unity of heart is crucial.

The Unification Church is at the forefront, facing the communist world under the banner of victory. We are in a position where we must be the first to be shot at and the first to sacrifice, even if it means suffering. We are currently engaged in such a struggle in Japan. We are fighting a battle where we do not know when or how it will unfold. Even when abroad, if one faces unjust persecution, it is the responsibility of their nation to stand up for them. That is why a nation is valuable. When one feels sorrow, it should not be merely their own sorrow but the sorrow of their nation, which allows them to stand up for the world.

The homeland is a serious matter. If one’s brothers are suffering abroad and one turns a blind eye, that nation is powerless and doomed. You, who are in the homeland! When you hear news from abroad, do not adopt a habitual and decadent mindset that considers it normal. Those who do so are indifferent.

When there is good news, should there not be a heart that can dance with joy even without eating? When sad news comes, should one not forget to eat and sleep, feeling the pain as if it were their own? Such a person is the true owner, the one who has become a son of the owner. Those who merely watch like a third party, laughing and speaking carelessly, are rebels who evoke the owner’s sorrow. If they are the enemies that need to be dealt with, they must be resolved first.

When considering these issues, now is the time for you all to unite and pray. We must prepare with sincerity for the 15 days leading up to August 15th. Where will unification be centered? It must be centered around heaven.

From this perspective, I urge you to truly become one family in heart. This is the time when such a heart is most needed. With a loving heart as family members, we must establish a tradition of liberating Christianity, which has been trapped in the hands of enemies and unable to walk the heavenly path, and of saving our nation.

Otherwise, where will they go? They cannot cross over to the Unification Church. Do you understand? The Unification Church must pass through them and present the ideal path they desire for them to be revived. The nation will not come to us. We must present a path beyond what the nation can take in order to save it. Only then will there be no adverse effects.

Thus, we come forth with anti-communism, and we come forth with sacrifice. We have entered an era where this can now manifest. When we engage in anti-communism, the Unification Church will be pointed out, and its activities will be highlighted. This is not in a negative sense; it will be evident that it is for the church, for the good God, and for the nation. Many churches will be able to see unification with joy, but if they try to come in, it will not be manageable. That means they will all perish. It cannot happen from an opposing position.

That is why God granted the liberation rights to Judaism and the Israelite people when the global fortune was centered around them, allowing them to follow at the right time. It is not that they achieved liberation on their own. Korea itself was the same, and our Unification Church leaders were the same, were they not? History praises happiness there, and such things are what we should be thankful for before heaven. We cannot be the motivation ourselves. We cannot lead ourselves. Because heaven has put us in the forefront to bring about this victory, we can always be grateful. We are always thankful. That is how it is.

In order for the Unification Church to be a church that can be grateful, it must not think, “Ah, the established church should bow to us.” Instead, it must create a better church and become more excellent sons and daughters of God, showing them an example and influencing them. When that happens, they will follow even if told not to, and in this way, we can completely save them. The same goes for the nation. We must go where the nation cannot go. That is why we have been engaging in such activities until now.

So, is this for the Unification Church, or is it truly for the nation? The nation senses that. Some people slander that the Unification Church is doing these activities to rise to prominence or to establish a political base, but it is not for the Unification Church. It is for the nation. When our position of acting for the benefit of the nation is revealed in broad daylight, the nation will… That is natural unification.

Thus, after completing the third world tour, what has the teacher been doing until now? He is doing what the world cannot do. That is how natural unification will unfold. Wouldn’t you agree?

Then, regarding yourselves, if you have families, your family must become the center before your tribe, doing what the tribe cannot do and working for the tribe’s benefit. Then they will naturally follow. This is the way of unification.

Therefore, parents hope that their children will become the center of a higher position in the future. A good child is not one who is only good for a day, but a child who has always been a source of strength and hope for their parents, even in difficult or sorrowful times. When such conditions remain, the parents will naturally follow that child. They will hand over everything they have, and even if they say they will not take it, they will want to pass it on; that is the custom of the heart.

When we think about these things, who will take on such responsibilities? Who will show an example before countless religions? The teacher cannot do it alone. Who will take on the responsibility to be an example before countless nations? The teacher alone cannot do it. We must do it, we must. Only here… And while caring for the family, for the whole, and ensuring that through me the family can be comforted, and with the heart to make the family comfortable, if we stand at the forefront, taking on all responsibilities and limping forward, tears of divine compassion will surround us. Such a person will not perish. They will never perish. You must understand that through them, a unifying environment will be established.

From this perspective, internal unity of heart is more important than external unification. 

Not at a place where heaven and tragedy are at odds, but at a place where they share in heaven, starting from the same place and the same heart, if a child thinks of their past disobedience before heaven, this is a good chance to be forgiven and liberated from the history of disobedience. If they can sacrifice themselves in that place, the blessings of heaven will be connected through them.

Through such people, I believe a path will emerge for the nation to receive heavenly fortune.

From this perspective, I hope you will truly become a family that is fulfilling, a mutual resting place of heart, and a direction of hope.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, as I recall the decades past, this body was unable to escape the fate of the nation.

Now I have spoken about what the members of unification should be like. The members of unification must achieve unity of heart. At the same time, we know the history of our disobedience, so before heaven can strike, I must be struck first.

*2) The Father’s Sorrow

<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is August 6, 1972, and on this first Sabbath of the month, may your protection, grace, and guidance be with us. We must sincerely thank you for leading us until now, despite our shortcomings.

Now that we have entered this new month, may it be a month where we truly give thanks and dedicate ourselves to you. Father, we wish to follow your will, but we often fail to prioritize you and instead prioritize ourselves, so please forgive us.

This morning, please remember your children who are bowing before you. We are aware of where we stand and know that we have a path to run toward the boundary of restoration that you have left us. We must not walk this path by anyone’s strength but must each carry our own cross and fight the final battle before you.

Father, who has patiently labored for us, we recognize your compassion for us, and when we realize that you cannot abandon us, we always feel your sorrow.

Father, this morning, as your children scattered across the nation look to this place, may you be with them in every corner. Especially during this period, as we unite our hearts around the nation and people, and with concern for the future problems of Asia, may you be with us in a special way during this time.

Father, may everything internal become one with your will, and may all external issues become a foundation of welcome before your providential will.

Whenever we think of you, who has labored for us, we feel our efforts are insufficient and our sincerity lacking. We are well aware that we must pledge to fulfill the mission of tomorrow’s pioneers, so we earnestly ask for your guidance.

This morning, in every place where your name is invoked, not only in Korea but also among your children scattered worldwide, may you be personally present, and especially remember the mobilization team. They are the first group to step out for heaven in history, so may their movement bear witness to your will, express your life connection, and reveal your existence, thereby glorifying you before all and expanding the foundation of your victory.

May your life force be present in every place where they are seen and where they connect with others, linking each individual’s heart. Thus, may they become an absolutely necessary movement in expanding the foundation of the Father’s victory nation and world, and may they become such a group.

This morning, please personally watch over all of us. All of our desires are your will. It is also the path you are fighting on, so may we inherit that struggle and become heavenly warriors to overcome the path of suffering.
I earnestly hope and wish that we may fulfill our duties. Father, may we respond on earth as you look down from heaven, and I sincerely ask and wish that what we request aligns with your will.

Glory of ten thousand years, I earnestly ask that we may achieve the day of your victory through our unity, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> There is no human being living on this earth who does not have a hope. Furthermore, it is human nature and instinct to strive with all loyalty and effort towards that hope. In other words, humans wish for something better than the present. It is the desire of humanity to wish for progress beyond the current situation.

The hope of God and humanity is to find happiness. From this perspective, we can understand that we humans were born resembling God. Since it is said that we were created in the image of God, if there is a God who is the essence, we too were created to resemble Him.

When we see that we have the heart to hope for a place where we can hold such hopes, we realize that we stand in a relative position rather than a purely subjective or motivational stance. This indicates that our desire to have such a heart is because we hope for a collective experience centered around a certain purpose that aligns with us. Because there is such a heart in some subject, we humans cannot help but have that heart as well.

From this perspective, if there is a God who is the subject beyond humanity, we can infer that God must also have a desire for something better, a higher ideal. In other words, we understand that God cannot help but pursue an ideal that is better than the current situation.

When we look at humanity, the hope that humans desire is not a place of unhappiness. If there is a nation that has fulfilled such hopes, its ruler would want to boast before all nations. Regardless of the size of their circumstances, whether in a small position or a large one, they want to express the hope they had to achieve their desires. This desire to express is not limited to their current environment but extends to nations and even higher places, revealing the human heart.

Just as humanity is like this, it is certain that God would want to boast about a place where His hopes are fulfilled. When we consider what God or humanity can boast about, there may be external matters to boast of, but the more central and core factor that they would want to boast about must be a place of happiness.

So what does a happy place look like? It is a place where one does not feel a lack in the whole. It is a place that is full both internally and externally, a place where there is nothing more to desire. When we think about this, a happy place is one where one can receive infinitely when they want to receive and can give infinitely when they want to give.

What does it mean to be unhappy? It means not being able to receive what one wishes to receive, or being in a position where one cannot give what they truly want to give. Therefore, a happy place is one where one can always give and receive, a place where one's relative environment can respond to their heart's desires. It is a place where, in all aspects of life, whatever one observes, the environment does not hinder their movement.

When we think about this, what is the center of desire? In considering this, we realize that where there are parents, there must be children. When there are no children before the parents, the happiness of those parents cannot exist. The joy of the parents cannot be realized. Likewise, when there are no parents before the children, the joy of those children is incomplete. We cannot help but think this way. Similarly, if there is a man, there must be a counterpart before him. The same goes for women. Therefore, when there is a couple, they must become one.

What should they unite around? In the relationship of subject and object, what is the mutual desire? It is centered around a higher love. In pursuing a more valuable and multidimensional love than the current position, and believing that it will surely be so from a practical standpoint, it is only in that place of mutual unity that we can stimulate tomorrow's happiness and appreciate today's happiness.

Moreover, when there is a couple, there must be children before them. In forming a family, there must be parents above and children below, as well as the couple themselves.

Thus, parents must unite with each other, and the couple must unite with each other. When looking at children centered around the couple, the children must also unite with each other. While this shows a vertical three-stage structure, horizontally, since there are pairs, we must consider that the six individuals must unite.

So, who should be the center of this unity? It cannot be just humans. Humans alone cannot pursue the highest ideals or higher values. Therefore, what is the one thing that must be present among these six individuals? We must recognize that we are limited beings. As beings who cannot go beyond our limitations, we exist in a relative position rather than an absolute one. For this reason, if there is something absolute, an absolute subject of love, then centered around that, parents would wish to become one, couples would wish to become one, and children would wish to become one. When we consider that parents, couples, and the new children born from that couple should become one, we see that without something to connect the happiness of the parents, the couple, and the children, there is nothing to link them.

To unify everything and integrate all into a more valuable position that is hopeful and stimulating, there must be something, and that is not just human love but absolute love. It is only possible when centered around that. From this perspective, if God has an ideal as the highest being, what would that ideal be? There cannot be a higher ideal than that. Once one reaches the highest position, they must come down. If one has risen, they must lower themselves. The universe operates on the principle of give and take. Therefore, if one has risen, they must come down, and if one has received, they must give. If there is a higher ideal that can exist before the highest love or absolute subject, we must consider where that ideal can be realized. It cannot be realized from a higher position.

No matter how absolute a position may be, if that absolute position stands in a higher place, then that absolute position must stand in a relative position. Otherwise, it cannot be a subject. We cannot overlook this. Thus, the absolute subject must inevitably pursue ideals for the sake of the relative.

No matter how wonderful a person may be, whether they are a world-renowned scholar, artist, politician, or even a highly esteemed saint, they cannot rejoice alone. Joy cannot be felt in solitude. Joy exists in a situation where relative conditions are met. Even the highest person, when viewed in relation to others, may find something higher to rejoice in, but if that is the highest position, they cannot rejoice centered around that alone.

If there is a highest position, that position must also require a counterpart. Therefore, we understand that one cannot rejoice alone. From this perspective, where will God's joy manifest? When we consider this, we see that joy arises not from seeking a higher position but because God, being the absolute being, is the end, the ultimate center, and thus must pursue that relative aspect.

When we observe any object, when sunlight shines, a shadow is inevitably cast. In the same manner, we cannot help but think that the subject must want to give not for the sake of something higher but for the sake of lower humans and all creation.

Why did God create the universe? It was to realize His ideals. From this perspective of ideal realization, we see a connection from the smallest creatures to great humanity. Of course, this includes the natural world, but God created from the smallest to the largest. So what is the smallest? The smallest is a part of everything that becomes a relative counterpart to God.

Because God created from the smallest with the absolute relative requirement, there is a starting point to love the small things. When one aspires to rise above the small, they would have felt a relative stimulation. They would have felt a progressively higher meaning of stimulation. This is undeniable. From the small to the large, this is how humanity was created.

What kind of existence is humanity? We are the sons and daughters of God. Since we were created as God's sons and daughters, God must have intended to realize ideal love centered on humanity. So, is there anything other than humanity? There cannot be. Can there be anything other than the relative? No. Therefore, because God wanted to love humanity, there cannot be an ideal that excludes love. Thus, God's ideal will be realized centered on love for humanity, and what kind of love is that? It is parental love when viewed from the perspective of God. From the perspective of humanity, the absolute God can love humanity as a parent and can love humanity as children. Therefore, the point of unity where God can love must be at a high position for growing humanity, not a low one. In other words, with the perfection of humanity, there must be a point of unity where they can stand confidently as children before the parental God and receive and give love.

From this perspective, what is the position of ideal love as a place of realization? If humanity had become the sons and daughters who could completely receive God's love immediately after being created, it might be different. However, all principles of creation must go through a process to achieve perfection, so humanity does not receive complete love from God immediately after creation. They must grow progressively to reach that love. Therefore, from the perspective of humanity, that position is a future place, a place of hope.

If humanity reaches that place, then they would have welcomed the position where both humanity and God can be happy. Moreover, the happiness felt by the absolute being and the love felt by the absolute being must be eternal. If one observes the origin of that love, it will be eternal, and if humanity has the authority to coexist with that love, then that authority and the place of coexistence cannot change. No matter what changes, the place aligned with God's absolute love cannot change.

How can we know this? We can understand it by looking at humanity. The place where I truly loved cannot be forgotten. It is something that cannot be taken away, something that cannot be conquered. Even if it were conquered, it manifests as self-liberation and autonomy, which we experience in our daily lives as fallen humans. In this light, our failure to reach the hopeful, ideal, and happy place, or our loss of it, is what we call the fall. Therefore, the hopeful, ideal, and happy foundation remains because it has not been reached.

Our inherent heart must have the foundation to reach that place to connect with the absolute ideal of God. If our nature does not aspire to that place, we can never reach the time of unity with it. Because there is an absolute God, our inherent heart must inevitably have the hope to align with it. Even if we have fallen, that stimulating hope remains within humanity, which is why we believe that through this heart, God can once again restore humanity and provide a path to salvation.

The sorrow of heaven and humanity caused by the fall. 

When we consider this, the question arises whether there are people who know of a place of love where they can truly unite with God, or whether there are people who have reached that place. 

If there were ancestors who reached such a place, it would have become a foundation of happiness for humanity, and the feelings and results of happiness from that foundation would have remained as a traditional fact in human history. However, that has not happened. Therefore, that place remains as a realm of unfulfilled potential before humanity today, as the content of the hope we pursue. Moreover, the absolute God has established an ideal place, a happy place, where our hopes can align in relation to humanity. If that standard is not absolutely fulfilled, the authority of the absolute cannot be established. Thus, even though humanity has fallen, it must be lifted up again.
The place that has returned to its original position cannot help but pursue the happy path. This is seen as the providential way for God to save humanity if God exists.

So, can we find the place of hope all at once? It cannot be done all at once; therefore, to restore this, we must go through the opposite process of having fallen down. This is an undeniable fact.

Now, what is the place that our original human beings should be in? As mentioned earlier, humans should have been born as direct children of God. If we were born as direct children, we cannot help but think that God would have loved us, centered on the parents and ancestors of humanity who did not fall.

Then, looking at the life from childhood to adulthood or old age, we may not know if God loved us in our childhood or youth, but did we live in the protection of God's love during adulthood and old age? When we affirm that we have fallen, the period after that fall is not within God's protective realm. It is outside of God's expulsion and protection. It is not within God's ideal realm. When we look at humanity, which stands in opposition to God, that place cannot be a place of happiness but must be a place of despair. Because it could not become a place of happiness, sorrow has arisen above to God, and below, humanity cannot help but feel sorrow; isn't this our life? This is beyond question.

The salvation of fallen humanity begins with complete disassembly.

Then, how far have we fallen? Have we fallen from the position of God's son to that of a servant? We have fallen even further. We have fallen to the value of a lump of dirt. If there is a product made in a factory, and that product is not made as envisioned by the creator but instead is a defective product, isn't it harder to remake it than to make it from scratch? We all know this well. To restore it to something new, we must completely disassemble it. Whether it is a large or small object, everything must be disassembled and reassembled. Here, we come to understand that we must pursue a new product that aligns with a complete design of parts.

In this light, if humanity has fallen, we must completely disassemble the fallen humanity to restore it. So how do we perform this disassembly? If there are parents, we cannot simply hold onto them to perform the disassembly; if there are spouses, we cannot just hold onto them; if there are children, we cannot just hold onto them. Therefore, the process of restoration, the providential process of God's salvation, begins with complete disassembly. Each individual must be whole.

When a perfect object is combined for a single purpose, it becomes a completed product. For a house to be completed, every part, including the doors and all associated components, must be perfect. Only then can a house be completed. When we consider this issue, we pursue a perfect individual. This is why Matthew 5:48 says, "Be perfect, therefore, as your heavenly Father is perfect." What is the standard? It is to be perfect like the perfection of heaven. Pursuing an objective value that can be close to the absolute is beyond question. If the owner has a certain design, shouldn't the product be made based on that design, perfectly aligned without any deviation? Similarly, God cannot help but pursue it from that standpoint. It demands perfection. How perfect does it demand? It requires a perfect product that is not ashamed to stand before the Absolute.

Then we must analyze our lives. We must tear apart our lives completely. We must also dismantle all our thoughts. <Words> We, who have gathered here, are a group that claims to be members of the Unification Church. The vast proposition of unification is not simply something presented for the desires or purposes of any individual.

Unification arises from serving the whole.
Unification occurs not by being led, but by leading, and can only be realized through seeking and presenting new solutions. In the current state of disunity, to achieve unification, we must transcend the present environment and seek and present another solution. Only there can unification be possible.

No one wishes for unification from a position of lack of freedom. No one desires unification from a position of insecurity. We know that it is the heart of conscientious human beings to wish for unification from a position of freedom and joy.

Then, if ten people gather, each should not have different wishes for unity. However, if there are ten people, each has their own opinions. If there are a hundred people, there are a hundred different opinions. If a thousand people gather, there are a thousand... In a free environment, when asked to assert themselves centered on themselves, there is no one who does not want to assert themselves.

Even when considering the entire population of 30 million in the Republic of Korea, each of those 30 million individuals thinks centered on themselves. We know that it is human nature to wish that their own thoughts can stand as thoughts that represent the whole.

When we think this way, it is the same not only for a country or a nation but also for humanity in the present age. Although many people live in this world, they also wish for something to be realized centered on themselves. Therefore, when 3 billion people wish for everything to be realized centered on themselves, the question arises whether this can bring benefits to the whole. When such wishes sacrifice the whole for the sake of the individual, no matter how excellent that individual is or how they assert themselves from the highest position, that wish cannot be fulfilled.

Only through accepting the will that the whole can be better can we seek a path, and we cannot help but think that the way for the whole to take on a unified form begins there.

Now, when we consider the countless people who have come and gone throughout historical times, did they not also wish for some great desire centered on themselves? Many people in the past have pursued a better and united world in their hearts, but we know well that the world they wished for was not realized. Among those countless people in history, we recognize that those who are somewhat better, those who are revered, are those who inherit the wishes, thoughts, and intentions of the saints.

Then, when we consider whether the wishes that those saints pursued can be realized in this world, we also know that this is nearly impossible. Many people in the past wished for such a will, but they could not realize it, and among the countless humans living today, while no one wishes for it, we must conclude that it is also close to impossible.

In light of these facts, we cannot help but worry about how humanity will be in the future.

The wishes of humanity hitting the wall of despair.
So, will the world of unity that we humans desire, a world of peace centered on freedom, come? Given that it was the case in the past and is the case in the present, we know all too well that such a world cannot be hoped for in the future.

All of humanity, or the world situation, remains in this predicament. Broadly speaking, there are democratic and communist worlds, but can these two worlds truly seek a unified world that all humanity desires in their hearts? We can also conclude that this is close to impossible. Furthermore, when we consider who will start this and where, we cannot help but conclude that it is impossible with just people alone.

Therefore, in the face of the turbulent global situation, it is time for believers to re-examine the essence of their faith. Politicians must also analyze and critique their human values centered on their essence. Economists and cultural figures, as well as people from all walks of life, must also critically reassess the global situation and reconsider the fundamental factors that pursue unity.

When we think this way, have we not exhausted all the thoughts that humans can have? Have we not reached the maximum limit of what humans can achieve? We cannot help but reach such a conclusion. When we come to that conclusion and return to the essence of humanity, we must ask ourselves if we can have any wishes there, and we find that we cannot have any wishes. There is only despair.

Then, in the midst of this despair, do we even have a belief or a self to overcome this? When we look at our past history or our current circumstances, we cannot help but discover that we possess nothing that can assure us of hope for tomorrow. 

From this perspective, if we conclude that it is impossible for our humanity, we are left with no choice but to face the wall of despair. However, that does not mean...
Have you found a new path to turn back and go? There is none. When we find ourselves standing in such a position, can the friends I like truly become good friends for tomorrow? Can the happy environment I currently live in, or the unhappy environment, pave the way for new aspirations and carry them forward into the future? At that moment, we discover a self that cannot have confidence in itself. When we think of ourselves like this, when we think of us like this, when we think of humanity like this, it is indeed miserable.

We do not have a foundation that can guarantee today, nor do we stand in a place where we can inherit new hopes for tomorrow. Isn’t humanity confronted with despair? We can feel this through various social conditions that we cannot ignore.

Then, if it is just people, it may seem hopeless, but what if there is something above people? We often ask, “Is that person good or evil?” We evaluate whether someone is a good person or a bad person, whether they are a good friend or a bad friend. When we look at it this way, was there ever a truly good friend? Was there ever a truly good parent? Was there ever a truly good sibling? When we focus on humanity, we wish that there is only truth, but we cannot find it. We want to stand in the true place, but we cannot stand in the true place.

What is that true place? We hope to stand there, but do we not know what kind of place that true place is? This cannot be a trivial matter. If I cannot stand in the true place, does that mean I am standing in an evil place? Then, what is the ultimate limit of evil? This too seems vague.

When we consider the two types of people who stand in the position of pursuing goodness, we find ourselves caught in the dilemma of being either good or evil. So, how do we seek that good position? There are no methods to explore. What should we do? We cannot all choose to go to an evil position. This struggle is what our lives are about.

Your life is precious. Your life is the most precious thing. In this regard, is it not true that today’s humanity is wandering without a clear path and decisive subjectivity? Then, who has ever stood at the point of humanity’s greatest desire and claimed that this is the decisive position of goodness that humanity should stand in? That too is not trustworthy.

When we consider these issues, is it not impossible to resolve our environment and pursue the direction of goodness? Standing in such a position cannot be a trivial matter.

You may have many such moments. 124   We Who Face the Will
If there had been a subject with the will proclaimed by God's love in the historical age, where would that love be realized? It can only be achieved through those who are willing to walk the path of God's love. It is certain. Once we know that God exists, it is undeniable. 
Does what I desire align with what He desires? Does my way of living align with His way of living? That becomes the issue. Because we are those who face the will, that is the problem. Is my situation more precious than His? Is the dimension of my heart higher than His? There is no need to ask. We are humans who cannot transcend the connections of the historical age. We are humans who cannot escape the relationships of historical circumstances. We cannot claim to be lives that transcend the world of connections and relationships, the world of cause and effect. If we discover a self that feels sorrow here and groan in pursuit of alternatives for overcoming, then that search for solutions is not within ourselves. If there is a new subject that worries about dealing with evil, would that not be an unspeakable good news? If we know that such a person exists, how much devotion should we give for that person? This is the issue.

When young men and women are captivated by the flames of first love, they rush toward that love without caring for life or death. If there is such a path of love, how strong would that path of love be? Would it not be impossible to block it with a sword or any authority? Even if one gathers the authority of all humans on this earth for a thousand or ten thousand years, would it not be impossible to block it?
