When he looks at the position he should originally stand in, the positions of God and Jesus, God and the Son, were misaligned. Do you understand? To do according to God's will is to go against human will, and to do according to human will is to go against God's will, so wasn't Jesus' life a struggle in that middle position?  
We are the same. When we try to do according to the will of the Unification Church, there are many obstacles from the world, and when we try to do according to God's will, there are many obstacles from humanity. If we do according to human will, what obstacles are there? Although the times are different, there are times that are connected, times that correspond relatively, and that is the time that our Unification Church desires. You need to understand this.  
In this sense, we must become those who face the will. What is the country I want to be proud of, the world I want to be proud of, the country Jesus wants to be proud of, and the world Jesus wants to be proud of? We must take that as our goal and leave a foundation of my past, present, and future that I can be proud of.  
Determined to give up my life and equipped with the heart of the fallen, we, who believe in the Unification Church, want to leave this path with the heart of the prophets of old. This is how we see it.  
Now, from that standpoint, you must reach that attitude.  
How many tears have you shed for your country, for your family, for your brothers? Have you truly loved? This is the issue. Because the Unification Church pursues a heart-centered history, we must not be lower than the heart of Jesus in the historical era. We must be higher, centered on God's heart. Now is the time of hope when Jesus can come, so we must become a solid foundation equipped with high-level content in our environment. Isn't this the lifestyle attitude of believers in the Unification Church?  
From this perspective, we must compare and critique our standards with ourselves today. Since the present is the issue, it is not too late even now. We must make a new start for tomorrow.  
Look, the people of Israel awaited the Messiah for 4,000 years, and when he came, he said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is near." John the Baptist also said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is near." The same goes for you. You must repent. You must repent for not being faithful to your country, for not being faithful to the will, and for not loving humanity. Thus, you must repent from one to the whole world. Is there any loss in repenting? Isn't that so? Can you lose anything by repenting? It is the same principle. You must also repent based on a principled standard. Only then will the kingdom of heaven come. You must move God through your repentance. This is where unity begins. (The following words are not recorded.)  
Let us become sons who love the will.  
This training center is truly beautiful. I named the mountain behind this training center. I called it Cheonseungdae (Heavenly Ascension Platform). I named the whole area Cheonseungdae.  
Cheongpyeong is a place that God has planned as important.  
So, this place has become like this. That mountain behind, that mountain is Cheonseongsan (Heavenly Holy Mountain). On the peak in the middle, I wrote the character for "holy," and on the peak over there, I wrote the character for "to accomplish," and on this side, I wrote the character for "castle." It is the Three Saints, Three Holy Mountains, where the middle represents "holiness," the other side represents "accomplishment," and this side represents "protection."  
How is that mountain? The mountain is aligned straight like a folding screen. When you look at this terrain, it is arranged like a folding screen. All the mountains are high, but they are aligned straight like a folding screen, so everything looks lush. Therefore, I thought that there shouldn't be a mountain higher than that mountain within ten miles. If the big mountain range beyond that mountain stretches and passes through Jangsan, it shouldn't be. So I went up...  
On August 17, 1972 (Thursday), at the Cheongpyeong Training Center.

I went up on July 10. When I went up, I saw that this mountain was unexpectedly straight. Indeed, it is truly beautiful. This is like a folding screen, and what does it mean? It is like a table in front of the folding screen, a table. It is like a table, and the water here represents all harmony. If you look at the water, it changes hundreds of times a day. Just wait and see. This symbolizes harmony. Harmony speaks of all hope, or it speaks of infinity, and it speaks of the prosperity of the whole. From this perspective, this place is a very auspicious location. Do you understand? Everything is like that.  
Interestingly, when I bought this land... I bought this land in May 1970. From the end of April to mid-May, the price per pyeong was only 17 won, just 17 won. It looked so good...  
Everyone, we held a training session in 1969, right?  
"Yes, it was in 1969." That's right. We held a training session over there. When we came here to see it, it was indeed a good location. So I thought that everything had to match, and after checking, it was a really good place. Generally, when people see it, they think it is a place where the northwest wind blows, hitting their faces. Ordinary people dislike cold places in winter. So no one thinks of this location. However, the place is wonderful.  
So the teacher set up a tent here and stayed for two years. While doing that, he started buying this place, and now we have almost bought it all. So starting from 1971, did we build a tent? Why did we build a tent? Because when someone tries to buy this land, they would put a stop to it. "Oh, this land is a place where the wind hits, so it is useless," and they would come and run away. (Laughter) It's true.  
Also, to grab this land, they said there were many brokers here. There were brokers everywhere, and if someone encroached on their territory, they would try to stab them. So we had to manage everything inside and out to start. Since Cheongpyeong is a tourist area, we had to collaborate with the locals and the military, saying, "If these merchants gather here, international guests will come in the future, so we need some approval." We created a broker association to make everyone necessary for us. This way, it became that you couldn't sell or buy land without our approval. Because of this, we were able to buy freely. Even now, we can't sell freely. We must get our approval...  
So, in a short period, we bought this vast area. It became that we signed a contract every two days on average. What we bought like that will probably be an unprecedented event in history. So now, we have about 1.2 million pyeong, which corresponds to the land of about 140 people.  
If we hadn't created such an organization, we would never have been able to buy the land. When you buy land in Cheongpyeong, since it is Cheongpyeong Lake, all the people in Seoul who own land nearby know it. So if any land is sold, the price of the adjacent land will definitely go up. So they ask for a price. However, do the wealthy people living in Seoul know which organization bought it and for how much? They just throw a few thousand pyeong for ten won or give a thousand won as they feel like it, so the land price increases exponentially.  
This place is such a region, but it is generally a necessary and appropriate area... The mountains you see here are all our mountains, and in the middle of that mountain, there is our mountain, and that high mountain is also our mountain. This is important; it is generally our mountain. That is why in Cheongpyeong... there are 40,000 pyeong across from the Niagara Hotel down there, about 60,000 pyeong in front of this mountain, and about 70,000 pyeong over there; we have secured all the important places.  
Therefore, if someone wants to create a resort in Cheongpyeong or build a villa, when they come in and look for a good place, it is all our land. (Laughter) That's right. Therefore, the current situation around here is that it is rumored that the Unification Church has tightly wrapped Cheongpyeong, whether knowingly or unknowingly.  
Also interestingly, because we engaged in such buying activities in a short time, there were many side effects. There were indeed many side effects. There were many opposing people...
Yes. So, among the people who oppose, they say four or five were taken to the spiritual world. Because of that, there are rumors saying, "If you oppose the Unification Church, you will be ruined." Therefore, from a spiritual perspective, it can be seen that God has already planned this place to be important in the future.

Another interesting thing is that they are trying to buy this land, which is evaluated at only 17 won per pyeong, but it belonged to a deputy manager of the Korea Daily. Such people bought this land with their dreams for the future. So when they say they will pay the usual price, they don’t sell. They set a price that is more than double and say they will buy it. When they bought it, they paid a few won each. If you check the price, it’s all obvious, but it goes for 17 won, and we were thinking of buying it for 38 won; I even thought about going up to 55 won. I thought I would negotiate and say I would pay 38 won, and they said, "Oh my, what kind of rice cake is this?" So we bought 140,000 pyeong at 38 won each. At 38 won... Now, how much is it going for? They are asking for 3,000 won. If you want it, they will sell it for 3,000 won. Then, it’s like a good business deal.

With this, we were going to hold a pastor's public hearing on July 12 last year, setting up a tent, but since it was the rainy season, we thought it would be tough to come and suffer in the muddy area, and that complaints would spread nationwide, so we had no choice but to start from July 1 and complete the training center by July 10. We painted for two days, so it was a house built in eight days. You see? When you think about it, building a house isn’t that hard. When people unite, it’s frightening. We worked on this while eating and sleeping for 24 hours.

When we were raising the slate, the contract had been made three days prior. However, the person in charge of contacting didn’t bring the slate until the last day. It was a big problem. The pastors were coming on the 12th, and if it wasn’t finished by then, everything would collapse. Who would you bring to help build the house? (laughter) It was a big deal. We had to create some kind of miracle. While I was running around, I pleaded that if they didn’t pay, they wouldn’t give the slate, and I rented a small boat and brought it to the training center at 11:30 PM. By the time we unloaded everything, it was around 2:30 AM. The boat owner said it was already late at night, so he decided to stay overnight. But when he came down in the morning, he saw that all the slates had been placed on the ridge overnight. (laughter) He thought that since it was raining, they temporarily placed them up there to prevent them from getting wet. But there wasn’t a single worker visible on the slates. So, within a few hours overnight, everything was completely set up. That’s why this house got nicknamed the "Goblin House." (laughter)

When you look at it, it looks good because it’s painted. If you see it, it looks flat, like a meditative table. (laughter) If you stand still and look, it matches. It’s true.

From that perspective, the teacher believes that this area can become famous worldwide in the future.

Cheongpyeong is the land desired by the spiritual world.

What’s interesting is, do you know Yoon Bosal? "Yes." Among you, some might know Yoon Bosal, but we Unification Church members have received a lot of education from that person. 

For the past 18 years, that person has been devoted day and night for the Unification Church. Even now, they go back and forth three or four mountains a day. They are going around the eight provinces, working hard.

You see? They don’t come empty-handed. What did you bring? They bring melons, rice cakes, cakes, and they absolutely don’t come empty-handed. Yoon Bosal is so excited doing this.

Since they are devoted, they know everything. They are watching what the teacher is saying right now. They also know if someone here, like that guy with glasses, is dozing off. The spiritual world is like that in the future. When you guys on the ground are passing by carelessly, it will pass by. You see? In the future, it will come to the point where everything, even the soles of your shoes, will be examined and shaken out. You see? "Yes." That person is currently the president of the Jogye Order’s congregation. They are boasting about having 500 members. However, there are still many complaints. No matter how much you shout about being a great monk or whatever, if you ask them if they have seen Buddha, they will say they haven’t. But when asked, ‘Have you seen him?’ they say, ‘Of course, I have.’" When they say they have seen him, and you ask, "How do you know?" they say, "If you don’t know, I will let you know. Buddha said you ate this and that at any time. You can’t move." (laughter) They say this is not what I see but what Buddha says, and when asked, "Is that so or not?" they say, "Uh-huh." (laughter)

Because of this, the Avalokiteshvara Bodhisattva has all the monks of the Jogye Order dancing in the old man's hand. When the old man says, "Come," they say, "Yes." Even among his disciples... When you look at what they are doing, it seems like nothing, but there is something frightening about it.

Sitting quietly, until we start serious prayer, that was for three years. Starting from 1970, they realized the operation in Japan was planned all night long... They know everything through the spiritual world. They completely stopped their own business for us. They have about 50 houses in Seoul. They closed all the various businesses they were running. They have farms in Singapore and Los Angeles, and they trade with foreign countries, so they have a lot of money. But they all stopped completely. They knew that if they tried to make money, everything would collapse at once. They know that. They stopped everything and said, "Put all your devotion into the Unification Church." The more they stop everything, the greater the devotion they put in, the more support it provides. That’s true. That means it’s been forgiven. They are very well-connected.

Until three years ago, whenever someone came to our church, they were all treated well. So, there was no one who didn’t know the high-ranking officials. For three years, everything was at a standstill, and since the Unification Church was the major player, there was a lot of opposition at one time. "What is this prayer thing?"

But when you actually come and see, there’s nothing, and when you see, if you go somewhere, you are wearing ragged clothes... When you go to the mountains, you can’t wear nice clothes. You have to look like a beggar, with soot on your face. When you see that, people say, "Wow, it’s true. It’s true." It spread as rumors... These days, it’s a bit quiet.

At that time, there were lines of people making tens of thousands of won a day. And all the business people, whether in international trade or doing big business, would bid for contracts worth tens of millions or hundreds of millions of won, and if they made a profit, they would definitely give a reward. So even now, making money is not a problem. What they say is that in the future, if they place themselves in Japan or New York, all the economic and political figures will be dancing in their hands. That’s how it has to be. They know everything clearly.

Now, regarding Yoon Bosal, when I bought this land and entered Cheongpyeong, they said, "Wow, today the spiritual world is dancing with joy." The old man is happy and dancing around, and when I arrived, he said, "Teacher, you signed the contract for the land today, right?" I did this and that today." Then he said, "Everything is like this, and what I said is definitely true." He was watching everything. The teacher met a certain introducer, and that introducer introduced someone who looked like a miser, and the owner is someone from the Korea Daily newspaper, and they know everything about what’s going on. Then he asked, "Even with all this, do you still say it’s not true?" (laughter) He was reporting this, giving a very surprising report. From that, it is undoubtedly the land that the spiritual world desired.

So we bought that land, and they said to buy the land in front of it. That land was originally intended for Americans to build vacation homes. The land in front has a good location. First, the view is good. But how much was the land price at that time? It went up to 17 won. But do the Americans know the price of this land? Compared to their country’s land prices, this is cheaper than a mad dog. Since they know this, a few hundred won is like a free meal. It doesn’t matter at all. But the introducers try to bring as many Americans as possible and negotiate well to make a lot of profit. So if they charged three times, they would take a third from the owner. So this is how they profit.

Given that situation, at that time, it was a land that didn’t cost much. They knew that, and they were looking for the owner, saying they would contract for 300 won. We were looking at 130 won per pyeong at that time. So we were trying to contract for 130 won, but they said they would sell for 300 won, so we decided to contract with them. The date for the contract was the day after tomorrow, but the American got a telegram from his hometown saying there was an incident and to return home. So what can you do? (laughter) So he went back. So can you trust an American? (laughter) Don’t trust Americans. You can’t trust them. That guy is a businessman; who knows when he will come back, whether it will take ten years, several decades, or forever? You see how hard it is for Koreans to go abroad? So we promoted that and bought everything. We negotiated the promise of 300 won down to 170 won, saying we couldn’t do it for 130 won, and we contracted for about 20,000 pyeong.

If we hadn’t bought this land, when we held the training session, the foreigners would come in front and ruin everything. But because we secured this land, no one can enter here. Names of the mountains and lakes around the Cheongpyeong Training Center.

From that perspective, you should know that this place is famous. The name Cheongpyeong is also good. Cheongpyeong (淸平). This means everything is completely settled, and a new start can be made... That noun is like that. When you say "Cheong," it means green, and when you say "Pyeong," it means flat at the same time. Isn’t that right? It means clear and flat. So all the preparatory work is done, and if we just set up the pillars, we can start anytime... That noun is like that. In the future, Cheongpyeong will become Cheonpyeong. (laughter) This is the name of the lake. Even so, don’t say that now. If it becomes Cheonpyeong Lake, it will be difficult. That time will come in the future.

We named the lake in front of the training center Cheonsim Lake (天心湖). This mountain is called Seoninbong (仙人峯), and the mountain over there is called Cheonseonsan (天善山), with "good" and "kind" characters. This will be the site of our original training center main building. There, the energy of devotion will be full, and except for special people coming from abroad, no one can enter. You see? It’s not visible from here.

This place is a location to nurture people from all over the world. In the past, it was the teacher's job to go to the Su-taek-ri factory. It was just about eating and then going to the factory. Do you understand? These days, where has that devotion moved? It has moved here. After eating, they want to come here. 

Everyone, if you come here and take a look quietly, this is truly a good place. Even when you pray, your prayers are answered well. There is nothing corrupt here. Evil spirits do not appear to oppose anything. Looking at that, it shows that this is a well-prepared land. 

Interestingly, when I was trying to lay the foundation here, Yoon Bosal said, "Ah, how does the teacher know to build a school there?" I had been planning to build a school there since a thousand years ago… Is there some big serpent here? A big serpent came here, knowing that the teacher would come a thousand years later, and offered it to the teacher, saying that the place it protected would be a place to nurture people from all over the world in the future. Somehow, the serpent was dancing and making a fuss, saying it was really good. (Laughter) When I tell such stories, it’s very interesting. Listening to them talk with such enthusiasm is truly enjoyable. You must understand that we are all moving in a way that can correspond to the principle of heaven and earth harmonizing inside and out. 

So where will the school be built? It will be built here on the home ground, but the teacher dislikes such things the most, like entering… This place is low, right? The reason we chose this place is that if we build higher than this, the training center will be completely overshadowed. If you look down, it gets heavily pressed, so we need to preserve that. Therefore, if we raise this just a little, it will fit well. However, trying to build a house here means we have to cut everything down, which is a huge task. So, we need to raise it one level, and from here, we will either build a road or do something to build the school higher. Then we will push down the entire middle of that mountain and create a road over there. There is a high peak on this mountain. From there, it comes directly in. This is a really good view. 

The gathering of fish in the lake symbolizes the gathering of people from the world. 

"Teacher, in the world, men like to catch and eat snakes, right? But Unification Church members are told not to eat snakes. Since you mentioned the serpent, it reminds me." (Mother) 

Unification Church members should not eat snakes. Why? Because even snakes must be liberated. We must liberate Satan, so that is correct. (Laughter) While it’s okay for worldly people to eat snakes and kill them, it is not good for Unification Church members to eat snakes. It becomes a condition. We must liberate all of that. That’s how we interpret it. It’s really interesting. 

That’s why I feel the same way. The teacher has fished in this lake until now, but now the desire to fish has completely disappeared. The fishing I did back then was for the purpose of catching people from the world. Do you understand? It was a history of fishing for the world. Spiritually, I did all that play to catch big fish, which means I fulfilled my wishes. So, until two years ago, I fished, but now I have completely stopped. This is already our land, and we built our house, so we shouldn’t catch fish in front of our house. So, if I catch fish here, I let them go. Isn’t that right? If you think it’s good to catch fish from your own pond, it won’t last long. (Laughter) 

They grow here and keep spawning, and they keep spawning… And what’s wonderful is that if you go to the pond between that mountain and the field, you will see a bunch of little fish swimming around. What does that mean? It symbolizes that there can be countless prosperities. "Come on over, come on over." (Laughter) That’s how it should be. So in the future, I will also provide bait to raise fish, and when a big one comes naturally, waving its tail and opening its mouth, I will feed it so it can swallow it whole. The gathering of fish in this lake symbolizes that the people of the world gather, as life is said to be a suffering in this world, and it symbolizes that all the people of the world gather. The fact that the little fish are swimming around indicates that this training center is expected to develop. (Excited) That’s how it is. Why am I excited? (Laughter) 

Let’s talk about something else. If you look closely, in a prosperous house, even if a dog poops, it does so in the corner of that house’s yard. But if the owner complains, "Oh, why do all the neighborhood dogs come to poop in my yard?" it means they are chasing away blessings. "Come on over and poop, come on." That’s how it should be. (Laughter) That’s how it is. Already, the mountains, the nature, and all the animals are like that. Don’t animals have things they like? If they were created for people, they would want to be drawn to people who are close to heaven, who have a nature and character close to their original nature, and they would want to harmonize with those people. This is the principle beyond creation. That’s why it should be that way. 

Everyone, to know whether the ministers in our Unification Church are fulfilling their responsibilities or not, you can immediately tell by looking at how many neighborhood people come and go around the church yard. Wherever the teacher goes, it’s always a feast. No matter where I go, it’s a feast. Even if I go to a lonely neighborhood, after three days, the neighborhood grandfather will come and sit down, asking, "Where did you come from?" They become curious and get a curious disease. Their hearts feel restless. Such things happen. Why does that happen? Why does it happen? It cannot be otherwise. Just as all insects gather towards the bright places in the dark of night, humans, the crown of creation, cannot be unaware of that. They cannot be unaware of it. There must be a kind of transmission. Because of that, the transmission of the heart feels a stimulus that unites the subject and the object. That stimulus does not destroy oneself but rather urges one’s hopes and guides them towards success, so naturally, they are drawn in. 

That’s why the way for the church to prosper is to first make the neighborhood children like it. If they don’t like it, it won’t work. We need to become friends with the children who have runny noses and make them say, "Oh, our teacher!" After that, it’s the grandmothers and grandfathers. If we only become friends with the children and the grandmothers and grandfathers, then all the neighborhood people will become our friends. That’s the principle. 

What do people like the most? Babies. What do they dislike the most? Grandfathers and grandmothers who are about to die. It’s the extreme opposites. Isn’t the movement of heaven to encompass the extremes? That’s the principle. Isn’t it? Therefore, if we try to become one with the children and have grandfathers and grandmothers come with their canes, play around, eat, and leave, then that place will become a prosperous place. If you all become friends with the grandfathers and grandmothers, and if the grandfathers and grandmothers become so fond of you that they can’t sleep at night, wanting to leave their nice yards and houses, and come to sleep in the church’s big hall, then that place, that organization, that person will prosper. That’s the principle. Do you understand? "Yes." 

For that to happen, it doesn’t just happen. You must keep the lights bright, bright. Children love to play the most. Isn’t that right? Children love to play the most, but if they abandon playing and come here expecting something, there must be something more fun than playing. Also, older people, those who are older, only think about food. "Oh, I wish I could eat something delicious." That’s what they think. If they forget about eating and come here, there must be something more than that. 

What could be more than that in this world? There is nothing in the world. What haven’t older people experienced in this world? They’ve done it all. What could be sincere for them? It cannot be anything else. There is no will of God outside of that. Children are the same. Children are innocent and sensitive. Especially their sensitivity to goodness is even more acute. They like things for no reason. It must be like this for the church to develop. 

People, forms, and heavenly nature. 

When you look at your own face and see your impression, there is a form in people. If you say, "My impression is that of an eagle," then how do you plan to disguise your eyes, nose, and face? There are also impressions like that of a raccoon, and each is different. There are also impressions like that of an ox. They all look like that. 

That’s why in Eastern philosophy, people are categorized by their zodiac signs: ox, dog, rooster, rabbit… Some people, like rabbits, perk up their ears and look at the sky, thinking, "Is the enemy coming…." And when the enemy comes, they just pull their tails back. Such people cannot prosper even if they try. This shows that everyone has a form. People with a raccoon form are destined to dig holes from the beginning, and those with a fox form are all cunning. There are differences like that. 

From that perspective, when I see people, I think, "Ah, that guy is this kind of person." They are really quick to sense things. That’s how it is. 

Therefore, if you have that form, if you are a raccoon, there are animals that match the raccoon. There are animals that want to create their own pack. Faith and Me
Faith is originally about believing and revering. Trust is something used in human society, but faith is something that occurs between humans and heaven, so it is about believing and revering.

When we look at the word "faith," it is made up of the character for "person" (人) and the character for "word" (言). What is this faith? It is not the word centered on God. It is the word centered on people. It is a word spoken with people at the center, and what kind of word is it? It is the highest word. Where does this highest word come from? It comes from among people, and where do people come from? They come from heaven. Therefore, the highest person is not difficult to reach heaven.

Thus, where does the word of a true person come from? The content of the word of a true person is different from the words of people living in our human society today. When we ask where the source of the highest human word comes from, it cannot come from a human who excludes heaven. That word must come through the heart of a person, and it comes when the heart and thought are in agreement. 

Therefore, you should not just think and speak. The words must come out when thought and heart are in agreement to be trustworthy words. Thought symbolizes heaven, and the heart expresses one's subjectivity. When heaven and heart become one and we practice according to the word, then thought, heart, and body become one. If we look at that, the results will inevitably appear through the three-stage process.

If we look at God's own creation process, there is also a principle of three stages when God speaks. First, there is God's thought, then it is expressed through the heart, and then the realization occurs. Through such three stages, creation is formed. Of course, when realizing the word, it cannot be done with just the heart. There, too, God must be at the center, and God's heart and God's body must become one. Only then, when we say, "Let it be so. This is how creation occurs," can creation be realized.

When we humans do something, just like what God created, the results of our work appear through the unity of body and heart. Even when we look at all social organizations today or our nation, to achieve something, it must first be expressed in writing. Writing is what represents speech. Isn't that so? Therefore, when we express the plans made in words in writing and practice according to those plans, the intended purpose will be fulfilled.

Thus, what era are we in now? It is the era of words, the era of communication. When the time comes that words can move the world, know that it is the end. When the words of humans can move the world, know that it is the end. Do you understand? Then what is moving the world now? It is politics and economics. Here, politics refers to the nation, and economics refers to the conditions of living. When these are moved through the words of humans, it is the end. The current global situation is being moved by social systems centered on political life and economic life. This is a global phenomenon.

However, when viewed from the perspective of humans, it is not the subject. It is merely a part within the planning rights of humans. Both politics and economics are relative conditions within the planning rights of humans, not subjective conditions. So what is the subjective condition? It is national policy. Everything changes when centered on national policy.

However, the forms of a nation's economy or politics are the same worldwide. The purpose of wanting to make a nation prosperous through politics and economics is the same, but the content of the policies is entirely different. Therefore, when the policy directions are aligned and politics and economic life are unified, it will become a unified cultural world. Thus, even if this world develops centered on political history or economic history, the standard will be achieved through the alignment of policy direction.

Then, what does that policy consist of? It is established from ideology. From where is that ideology established? It is established from thought. Where does thought come from? It is established from higher-level spirit. This is how it works.

Ultimately, because humans started from spirit, the ideal world can only unfold when the spirit is directed accordingly. Joy comes only when things happen as thought dictates. For that thought to be realized, the heart and body must become one. In other words, thoughts are realized through people like me. This is the phenomenon facing the entire world today.

So how will the future world be? Just because political forms are established does not mean the world will unite, nor does it mean the world will unite just because economic living systems are the same. The world can only unite when policy directions become one. Where do conflicts or breakdowns between nations originate? They originate from differences in policy direction. It is because of those differences that the world collides and divides. Ultimately, it is because thoughts were different. Therefore, we must integrate those different thoughts.

Then, in integrating that, can it be done through human-to-human living, or can it be done centered on God? There are only two paths. However, even if humans integrate with each other, humans have desires to assert their own interests, claim their own authority, and pursue benefits only for themselves, so such humans with these desires cannot find ideals.

If a nation sets a policy and claims benefits centered on that policy, it will try to globalize it. Therefore, policies and ideologies established on human desires cannot pursue a single policy direction or a single line. Thus, what is being said here is that without discovering a path to recreate the stage of life through a system of thought related to absolute thought and absolute spirit, we cannot seek a unified world and cannot achieve a world of peace.

That is why until now, religion has been an enemy to the economic sphere and also an enemy to the political sphere. The world cannot be the same as heaven. Matter cannot be the same as heaven. Ultimately, what does that mean? It means to unify the spiritual direction of this world, and thereby establish national policies, and when the elements of politics and economics or the lives of the people adapt to that national policy, only then will the foundation of the earthly world that heaven desires be established.

What we call faith is to pursue the character of a true person centered on that character. Living while pursuing such a character is the life of faith. When we look at the character for "faith," it consists of the character for "person" (人) and the character for "word" (言), and the character for "to revere" (仰) also uses the character for "person" (人). This also does not exclude people. It is a path that goes forward centered on people. To revere means to center on an object of respect rather than oneself. From that position, we pursue the true word and aim to establish a direction through that word, which is the life of faith.

God is absolute and has one thought, so the world of faith must naturally be absorbed into God's one thought. Higher-level thought establishes a system by absorbing lower-level thoughts. This is the result of going through a main stream and entering the great ocean as a unified result. At that time, it must go in one direction.

To turn a cucumber field into a cabbage field, you first harvest all the cucumbers and then plow the cucumber field. If there is someone who is also good at sewing, then they must do even more. When a person is poisoned, there is nothing they cannot do. In that way, within three years, everything can be made clear and the path can be paved. If that happens, a daughter-in-law can enter that house and take control of everything, becoming the owner as well. Do you understand? If you make a three-year plan, it can definitely be done.

If you go to a village to evangelize, you can completely take over that village within three years and create a stronghold. It's not that you can't do it; it's that you are not doing it. You should try until the end and then say it can't be done; just sitting around and complaining without trying will not work. God will not help such people. You must do everything, and only then will you receive help. When you have tried everything and are about to give up and turn back, that is when you will receive help. That is how God works. Knowing this, when you return this time, you should criticize your past life and spend at least 80 percent of your time dealing with people. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Even if you skip three meals a day, you should speak more than three times about the Word. You need to talk a lot. If you talk all day, your tongue will swell. Even then, as you continue to speak, your tongue will keep getting bitten. You need to experience this as well. If your mouth swells, your lips will keep getting bitten. So when you try to eat, it won't go down your throat easily. That is all your own property. God remembers those things. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

You guys don’t want to lecture, do you? Aren't you the ones who don’t want to lecture? Do you dislike it, or do you like it? "I like it." What do you like? How much do you like it? Do you like it more than eating? Do you like it more than having a meal? "Sometimes." Then that means there are bad times, right? (Laughter) If you like it, how much do you like it? Should you like it more than meals or less? "I should like it more." Even if you skip three meals a day, you should speak more than three times. Even if one person comes, you should lecture. If you have eaten one meal, you should hold onto one person and pay for that meal, right? Don't you dislike that? If not, you are a thief. Such a person should be a fertilizer bin or a trash can.

Have you ever lectured more than three times a day? Holding onto three people… When you eat, don’t you say, "Oh, this is delicious, oh, this is delicious, oh, this is delicious"? When hungry people eat, it’s a mess, right? But when you come in hungry and there is no food, how desperate is that? You are desperate because there are no family members, right? How bad is the famine? So were you spiritually hungry or not? Were you full or hungry? "Hungry." Then, while saying the food is delicious physically, won’t you eat the spiritual food through the Word? When you deal with family members and people, it should be more fun than when you eat.

When you wake up in the morning, you should think, "Where should I go to preach today?" Just like a nursing mother looks for her baby, you should worry. Should I go to this house or that house? You should pray, "God! I am going to evangelize today, but I don’t know where to go." If you really don’t know, you can cast lots. You can spit on your palm and hit it, and wherever the biggest droplet falls, that is where you should go. (Laughter) That is correct. Casting lots like that is correct. Such things happen repeatedly. Ah, my thoughts are close to God’s thoughts… I am not a fortune teller, but I discover that what I am doing is close to God. God teaches us.

When you don’t know which house to go to on the roadside, just take a pen and say, "If the pen goes to the left, it’s this house, and if it goes to the right, it’s that house." Then decide. (Laughter) Then kick it and see where it goes. If you kicked it in the middle and the pen goes to the right, then you go to the right. (Laughter) That is correct. You need to play this game of applying your intentions to your environment practically. This is how you will feel it. Do you understand?

Our Hyojin, when he was in elementary school, always rode in a jeep. Since he always rode in a car, he couldn’t find his way alone. How would he know where the central government building is? But when the jeep didn’t come, he had to go home but didn’t know where to go. So how would he go? At that time, he thought, "Isn’t God there? If I don’t know, God is there. If I pray and go, it will be fine." So at the fork in the road, he prayed, "God! Which way should I go?" and thought, "I should go this way," and ended up at home. That’s how it is. Oh, when I pray, God will surely move my heart. That is the principle.

When Eve was about to fall, if she had sincerely asked, "God! The archangel says to do this, what should I do?" would God have remained silent? At that time, God could have taught her. When Eve had a pure heart and believed in God, if a child like that were to ask, it would be a big deal, and God would quickly answer her. That is why Hyojin’s teacher evaluated him as "Hyojin is a faithful child." He understood that he could pray to God.

Our Injin is also interesting. When going to Cheongpyeong at night, you need to wear a buoy. At that time, I asked, "If I throw you in with the buoy, do you think you can cross over there?" and he said, "I can cross." He said he could cross even if it was all night. I asked him if he wasn’t scared because it was a scary place, and he said, "What is there to be scared of? God is here." Seeing that, I thought, "Wow, these kids have such faith." What about you? Try doing it. It is correct. Such things keep happening.

When you go to bed at night, you should pray, "Father! I entrust my path for tomorrow to you, so please guide me in the direction I should think of as soon as I wake up." Then when you wake up in the morning, you will feel, "I should go this way." And sure enough, when you go, there will be someone waiting for you. Do you understand?

By doing this, you can develop your spiritual heart. When that happens, your thoughts will keep aligning. You will keep having thoughts like, "Today, this will happen." Unexpectedly, when a thought arises from a motive that is not yours, you must watch it closely. If you do, you will realize it was a revelation. This is how it works. I hope you develop that aspect and move forward.

After eating one meal, you should speak once about the Word, right? Do you understand? "Yes." At the very least, you should either eat spiritual food or feed someone so that you are not ashamed in front of a meal. Let’s keep this promise this time. You must earnestly preach to at least three people a day. Do you understand? "Yes." Don’t just ask people to come to the church. Before asking them to come, create a motive that makes it impossible not to bring them. On the day you regain your footing, your foundation will develop significantly within a few months. The time is also such a time. Do you understand? So don’t leave it to anyone else. Does a priest just leave his altar to someone else? How precious is the position of a priest?

If you are in a direct and close relationship with God, don’t worry if you haven’t prepared a sermon. That kind of training is also necessary. When I meet a famous person, I sometimes talk ten times a day. At that time, depending on the location, I must tell completely different stories. But do I prepare all of that? At that time, the heart is completely aware of being a sacrifice. The awareness of being a sacrifice… "I" does not exist. There is no consciousness of existence. There is no sense of ownership. It is a place of complete dedication.

That place is a solemn place. Those who stand before the sacrifice must bow their heads; that is the heavenly law. Do you understand? "Yes." At that altar, God is present and intervening. When you say, "Today, in front of this altar, I dedicate all my passion, all my strength, and all my efforts," and when you open your mouth with all the sincerity you have in your life, God will help you. Do you understand? A sacrifice is offered in a serious place.

That is why, with a serious heart that has never existed in your life, when you say, "This body dedicated before God, please use it as you will," and you have the heart of a sacrifice, God will always be with you. Then, by offering the necessary sacrifices at that place, you will receive grace, you will be able to receive atonement, and you will be able to speak words that correspond to that person. Do you understand? You already know. You know when you open your mouth.

If you live like that, the relationship between God and you will enter a realm that needs no explanation. That is how you will be able to develop wherever you go. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The question is how many people have been moved by the sermon you delivered with the heart you poured into your prayer. It must not be zero. Even if there are just three people who received grace, if God is with you, it will be more than ten times, hundreds of times more. The Bible says it will be a hundredfold, sixtyfold, thirtyfold, right? That is how it multiplies. Even if the numbers are like that, it is scientific. It is recorded in data, and God will surely work with undeniable weight. Do you understand? "Yes." That is why I say to pour your heart into it. The question is how much cooperation God gives when you preach to someone. When you preach in a serious place, that word becomes a word that represents God. Do you understand? "Yes."

And you must always be careful about which direction the teacher is going through right now. Matching your steps to that is the best way for you to see effectiveness in your preaching. It becomes a motive for bestowing gifts. You need to know what the teacher is doing right now and what mission he is directing, and you need to raise your heart to align your emotional standards with the teacher’s heart. When you move from a relative position in front of the teacher, heavenly fortune will come to you.

Let’s show the greatest record since entering the Unification Church. 

When the subject and object completely exchange, reproduction occurs, right? "Yes." The subject is not you. It is God. Since you have no direct way to communicate with God, the teacher is bridging that gap. Therefore, when you know what the teacher is doing and what mission he is directing, and you always center yourself around that, establishing yourself in a relative position of give and take, God will be with you. That is why I say to value official documents. Do you understand? "Yes." That is also why I say to value the publications sent from the headquarters.

What kind of people love their country? Those who feel a sense of foreboding about the future more than anyone else and create a foundation for countermeasures in that direction are patriots. If such people exist, that nation will rise. That is why you should always think about what path heaven should take in the future and say, "May God be with me and teach me that path." You should know what the teacher is doing now and what he will do in the future. A person who knows that and prepares in advance cannot help but be a filial child before their parents and a loyal subject before their country.

The question is how you relate that faith-based experience to your living environment. Relationships cannot be formed without connections. You must understand that those connections cannot be established without the connection between the teacher and you.

So what is the current intention? It is to gather people. Isn’t that right? It is the time to recruit citizens for the founding of a nation. It is the time to recruit a new army to establish the kingdom of heaven. How serious is that? That is why you are told to love God with all your heart, all your mind, and all your character.

Is it time to eat? We need to eat and gather again. Today, the discussion has become extensive around the issue of faith.

Now, when you return, you are being told to do enough that the teacher doesn’t have to worry anymore. If you are over 30 and approaching 40, isn’t it an age where you can believe without hesitation? Isn’t that right? "Yes." Now, raise your hand if you will not cause the teacher any more worries. Are you sure? "Yes." Haven’t you done all sorts of things to evangelize 120 people until now? Isn’t that right? That is the first evangelization operation, and then it goes into the second mobile unit operation. You must do whatever it takes centered around that. You cannot not do it. That is why we are currently conducting mobile unit training to create standards that can prevent failures. Next, we are conducting a movement to gather 500 people for the Principle Research Association. Do you understand? "Yes."

From now on, we need to change the gasoline tank and put gunpowder in it and light it. That is the teacher’s thought. If that happens, you will be in trouble. That cannot happen, so I hope you will return with the resolution, "Now, I will set the greatest record since entering the Unification Church. Let’s show our abilities to make that happen." Do you understand? "Yes." Will you do it or not? "I will." Raise your hand if you will do it. Put your hands down.

<Prayer> Beloved Father! When I think of the people gathered here, who you have called as important leaders to restore the nation, the world, and the universe through your history, I feel ashamed. Father, I am ashamed. Truly ashamed.

However, regarding your heart’s world… There are many talented people and great nations on this earth, but those people and those nations are rebelling against you. They are a group that is dying and fleeing, but they kneel before you, exhausted, crying out with their faces turned toward you, longing for you and striving to establish your nation. Because this group is in such a position, even if you stand in a pitiful position, you cannot abandon them.

Father, who has led history with sorrow until now! I know you must have felt even more sorrowful when you looked at our sad state. However, now these people have sworn before you to clear away all your worries and fulfill their future mission, so please protect their path.

You must look upon the future history centered around their families with compassion. You must be with them. When heaven departs, no shadow will remain. You have believed and come.
When your steps lead to distrust, you will inevitably come to think that no one suffers more than you do, and once again, you will feel that this place is a fearful and trembling one.  
We are infinitely saddened by the past when we became those who impose debts upon heaven by establishing ourselves. Today, we feel fear in our hearts, worried that we might become people living in a place that imposes debts upon heaven. We must become the worthy sons who can cover the debts of heaven and bear the burdens of heaven, and we must become the worthy family.  
Then, when we think that our descendants can receive the gifts of hope under your love and protection in the future, we are reminded that the path we must take is one where we must die for our purpose. We know that the Father, who watches over us as we stay up all night for the country and struggle for the world, sheds tears for us. We also know that only when we take the lead in finding the country can the Father take the lead in finding the world on our behalf. We understand that the fulfillment of the Father's wishes cannot be achieved in the future until the serious matters explode, and we have not yet reached the standards of misery that we must endure. We have not yet received all the arrows of persecution that we must experience.  
Because we have not been able to present ourselves as those who can boast before the world of Satan as inheritors of your faith and single-mindedness, we know that the Father's heart, which remains in the place of adversity while looking toward the desired country, is filled with resentment and sorrow. We earnestly ask and wish to become your sons who can sympathize with the Father, who has suppressed that heart and has come out to seek and wait.  
Father! We are now starting again toward the eight provinces and rivers. The appearance we have when we return must be different from the appearance we had when we came, and we must become children who can struggle to long for you. If the time to meet you is in the morning, we must long for the morning; if it is in the daytime, we must long for the day; if it is in the evening, we must wait for the evening. If that time has passed, then even at night or while sleeping, we must sleep with the single-minded desire to meet you. As someone who knows your wishes and has received your secret mission, we must become sons and daughters who want to be remembered in your heart and to be proud of in your thoughts by pioneering the path of the vanguard. Even if we collapse while trying to find you, if you protect us and if we can become those whom you, with a higher character and ideals, can bless, I know well that even if the world perishes, that group will not perish.  
When we think that the path to unification continues through a miserable road of tradition, we realize that a person bearing a serious responsibility is indeed a pitiful person. Even if he has a wife, he cannot love her freely, and even if he has sons and daughters, he must walk a path where he cannot love them freely, worrying that he might incur debts before your will and go against your wishes…  
How pitiful are these people on the earth? If there are such groups, you… (The rest is not recorded.)
